```mermaid
flowchart TD
    Start([start]) --> ParseArgs[/"parse_arguments()"/]
    ParseArgs -->|uses| Argparse[argparse]
    Start --> GetDBs[/"components.get_db_instances(stage)"/]
    GetDBs --> DBLoop{for db in prod_b_dbs}
    DBLoop --> CreateDB1[/"monitors.create_db_monitors(..., CPUUtilization, Average, 90000000000, True)"/]
    DBLoop --> CreateDB2[/"monitors.create_db_monitors(..., CPUUtilization, Average, 50000000000, False)"/]
    DBLoop --> CreateDB3[/"monitors.create_db_monitors(..., FreeableMemory, Average, 500000000, True)"/]
    DBLoop --> CreateDB4[/"monitors.create_db_monitors(..., FreeableMemory, Average, 2000000000, False)"/]
    DBLoop --> CreateDB5[/"monitors.create_db_monitors(..., FreeStorageSpace, Average, 1000000000, True)"/]
    DBLoop --> CreateDB6[/"monitors.create_db_monitors(..., FreeStorageSpace, Average, 10000000000, False)"/]
    CreateDB1 --> DBLoop
    CreateDB2 --> DBLoop
    CreateDB3 --> DBLoop
    CreateDB4 --> DBLoop
    CreateDB5 --> DBLoop
    CreateDB6 --> DBLoop
    DBLoop --> GetMonitoredLambdas[/"components.get_monitored_components(stage, 'lambda')"/]
    GetMonitoredLambdas --> PrintMonitored[/"print(monitored_lambdas)"/]
    PrintMonitored --> GetAllLambdas[/"components.get_lambdas(stage) -> all_lambdas"/]
    GetAllLambdas --> GetTelematics1[/"get_lambdas_from_service(stage,'tritrack')"/]
    GetTelematics1 --> GetTelematics2[/"get_lambdas_from_service(stage,'p44')"/]
    GetTelematics2 --> CombineTelematics[/"telematics_lambdas += ..."/]
    CombineTelematics --> CalcNeeded[/"lambdas_need_monitoring = all_lambdas - monitored_lambdas"/]
    CalcNeeded --> PrintAll[/"print(all_lambdas, len(all_lambdas))"/]
    PrintAll --> LambdaLoop{for lambda_name in all_lambdas}
    LambdaLoop --> CheckConsumer{if 'consumer_' in lambda_name}
    CheckConsumer -->|yes| SkipLambda([skip])
    CheckConsumer -->|no| IsTele[/"is_tele = f'{stage}-{lambda_name}' in telematics_lambdas"/]
    IsTele --> CreateLambda[/"monitors.create_lambda_monitors(stage, lambda_name, is_tele)"/]
    CreateLambda --> PrintCreated[/"print('Monitor created for', lambda_name)"/]
    PrintCreated --> LambdaLoop
    SkipLambda --> LambdaLoop
    LambdaLoop --> End([end])
    Start -.-> ExceptionHandler[/"except: print traceback, raise"/]
```

## Diagram 2

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class script {
        +parse_arguments()
        +main
    }
    class components {
        +get_db_instances(stage)
        +get_monitored_components(stage, type)
        +get_lambdas(stage)
        +get_lambdas_from_service(stage, service)
    }
    class monitors {
        +create_db_monitors(...)
        +create_lambda_monitors(stage, lambda_name, is_tele)
    }
    class argparse
    class traceback
    script --> components : uses
    script --> monitors : uses
    script --> argparse : imports
    script --> traceback : imports
    components ..> monitors : provides identifiers
    monitors ..> components : reads configuration/state
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant User
    participant Script
    participant Components
    participant Monitors
    participant Argparse
    participant Traceback
    User->>Script: run script with stage arg
    Script->>Argparse: parse_arguments()
    Argparse-->>Script: args
    Script->>Components: get_db_instances(args.stage)
    Components-->>Script: prod_b_dbs
    loop for each db
        Script->>Monitors: create_db_monitors(... CPUUtilization / FreeableMemory / FreeStorageSpace ...)
        Monitors-->>Script: created
    end
    Script->>Components: get_monitored_components(stage,'lambda')
    Components-->>Script: monitored_lambdas
    Script->>Components: get_lambdas(stage)
    Components-->>Script: all_lambdas
    Script->>Components: get_lambdas_from_service(stage,'tritrack')
    Components-->>Script: telematics_tritrack
    Script->>Components: get_lambdas_from_service(stage,'p44')
    Components-->>Script: telematics_p44
    Script->>Script: combine telematics, compute lambdas_need_monitoring
    loop for each lambda in all_lambdas
        alt lambda starts with consumer_
            Script-->>Script: skip
        else
            Script->>Monitors: create_lambda_monitors(stage, lambda_name, is_tele)
            Monitors-->>Script: created
        end
    end
    Script-->>User: finished or raise Traceback on exception
```
